108a8('bum): myi dmyigs/ phyi ma'i mtha' myi dmyigs// dbus su myi dmyigs so// ke'u shi ka chos rgya che ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di rgya che ba yin te/ de ci'i phyir/

108b2('bum): chen po rnams kyi pha rold tu phyind pa 'di rgya che ba yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de ni 'di ltar myig gi rnam par shes pa'i sngon gyi mtha' myi dmyigs/ phyi ma'i mtha' myi dmyigs/ dbus su myi dmyigs so//

108b8('bum): rol tu phyind pa 'di rgya che ba yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de ni 'di ltar lus kyi rnam par shes pa'i sngon gyi mtha' myi dmyigs/ phyi ma'i mtha' myi dmyigs dbus su myi dmyigs so//

110a2('bum): dbus myi dmyigs so// ke'u shi ka yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyend kyis tshor ba rgya che ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di rgya che ba yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka/

110a8('bum): kapha rol tu phyind pa 'di rgya che ba yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de ni 'od ltar rlung gi khams kyi sngom gi mtha' myi dmyigs/ phyi ma'i mtha' myi dmyigs/ dbus myi dmyigs so// ke'u ni ka nam mkha'i khams rgya

110b5('bum): byed rgya che ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpal sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di rgya che ba yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de ni 'di ster 'du byed kyi sngon go mtha' rgya

110b8('bum): sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di rgya me ba yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka don 'di ltar mying dang gzugs sngon gi mkha' myi dmyigs/ phyi ma'i mthal myi dmyigs/ dbus kyi myig sa
111a1('bum): ke'u shi ka skye mched drug rgya che ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di rgya che ba yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u ni ka de ni 'di ltar skye mched drug gi sngon ka/

111a4('bum): pha rol tu phyind pa 'di rgya che ba yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi/ ra ka de ni 'di ltar tshor ba'i sngon gi mtha' myi dmyigs/ phyi ma'i mtha' myi dmyigs/ dbus myi dmyigs so// ke'u shi ka sred

111b1('bum): dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di rgya che ba yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shrI ka de ni 'di ster skye ba'i sngon ga me bal myi dmyigs/ phyi ma'i mtha' myi dmyigs/ dbus kyi dmigs so

111b3('bum): mtha' myi dmyigs dbus myi dmyigs so// ke'u shi ka sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyi rid pa rgya che ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyi rid pa 'di rgya che ba yin te/ de ci'i byor/

111b8('bum): kyi pha rol tu phyind pa rgya che ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di rgya che ba yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de ni 'di ltar brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin
112a1('bum): pa'i sngon ka mtha' myi dmyigs/ phyi ma'i mtha' myi dmyigs/ dbus myi dbyigs so// ke'u shi ka bsam gtan ka pha rol tu phyind pa rgya che ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' rjen
112a2('bum): po rnams kyi pha ros tu phyind pa 'di rgya che ba yin te/ de ci'i byor zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de ni 'di ltar bsam ga ta gi pha rol tu phyinang pa'i sngon go mtha' myi byugs/ phyi ma'i mtha' myi dmyigs/ dbus kyi dbyin

112a5('bum): rnams kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di rgya che ba yin te/ de ci'i phyirazhe na/ ke'u shi ka de mi 'di ltar nang stong pa nyid kyi sngon ga mtha'amyi dmyigasaphyi ma'i mtha' myi dmyigs/ dbus myi dmyigs

112a7('bum): mapa' myi dmyigs/ snga ma'i miba' myi dmyigs/ dbus myi dmyigs so// ke'u shi ka phyi nang stong pa nyid rgya che ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'drin
112a8('bum): che ba yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de ni 'di ltar phyi nang stong pa nyid kyi sngon gi mtha' myi dmyigasaphyi ma'i mtha' myi dmyigs/ dbus myi dmyigs so// ke'u shi ka stong pa nyid stong pa nyid rgya che ba
112b1('bum): kyi byung chub sem sa pa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi pa sdud tu byinid pa 'di rtse me ba yin te/ de ci phyir zhe na/ ke ga ka de'i 'di sar slong pa nyid kyi sngo kyim mi dmigs/ phyima'i sa skye
112b2('bum): tho stong pa nyid kyi sto kim tha' gyi dmyigs phyi ma'i maya mya dbyigs/ dbus kyi dmyigs so// ke'u shi ka don das pa stong pa nyid rgyal ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' cher po rnams kyi rom
112b3('bum): tu phyid pa 'di rgya che ba yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhen/ kelu kete ni 'di ltar dron ngas pa stong pa nyid kyi sngon ka mema' myi dmyigs daphyi ma'i mtha' myi dmyigs/ dbus kyi dmyigs so// mun ka/ 
112b4('bum): 'dus byas stong pa nyid rgya che ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sem sa dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di rgya che ba la na te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de ni 'di ltar 'dus byas

112b6('bum): rol tu phyirid pa 'di skye che ba yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhen/ ke'u shi ke de'i 'di ltar 'dus byas stong pa nyid kyi sngor kayeba'i myi dmyigs/ phyi ma'i mtha' myi dmigs/ dbus kyi myigs so// ke'u ni kam
112b7('bum): las 'das pa stong pa nyid rgya che ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyi rang pa 'ang rgya che ba yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de ni 'di ltar mtha' las 'das pa stong pa
124a1('bum): tshad kyang dmyigs su myed de/ nam mkha' tshad myed pa'i phyir sred pa tshad myed do/ sred pa tshad myed pa'i phyir shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa tshad myed do// ke'u shi ka le nad pa tshad myed pa'i phyir byang chub
124a2('bum): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di tshad myed pa ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de ni 'di ster lend pa'i tshad ni dmyigs su myed do// ke'u shi ka 'di lta ste dper na nam mkha'i tshad
124a3('bum): ni dmyigs su myed do// ke'u shi ka de bzhin du le nad pa'i tshad kyang dmyigs su myed de/ nam mkha' tshad myed pa'i phyir le nad pa tshad myed do// le nad pa tshad myed pa'i phyir shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyi ring pa tshad myed do
124a4('bum): ke'u shi ka srid pa tshad myed pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sem nyes dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'ang tshad myed pa ste/ de ci'i phyire zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de ni 'di ltar srid pa
124a5('bum): tshad ni dmyigs su myed do// ke'u shi ka 'di lta ste dper na nam mkha 'i tshed ni dmyigs su myed do// ke'u shi ka de bzhin du srid pa'i tshad kyang dmyigs su myed do// nam mkha' tshad myed pa'i phyir
124a6('bum): srad pa tshad med do// srid pa tshad myed pa'i phyir shes rab kyi pha ro khang tu phyi nad pa chad myed do// ke'u sho ka skye ba tshad myed pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyinadu byang
124a7('bum): tshad byed pa skye / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u ni ka de ni 'di ltar skye ba'i tshad ni dmyigs su myed do// ke'u shi ka 'di ltar ste dper na nam mkha' tshe me dmyigs su myed do// ke'u ni ka de bzhin du skye ba'i ched
124a8('bum): sem su myed de/ nam mkha' tshad myed pa'i phyir skye ba tshad myed do// skye ba tshad myed pa'ibyor shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa tshad myong ngo // ke'u ni ka rba zhi tshed myed pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems
124b1('bum): po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di tshad myed pa ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de ni 'di ltar rga shi'i tshad ni dmyigs su myed do// ke'u shi ka 'di lta ste dper na nam mkha'i tshad dade dmyigs
124b2('bum): su myed do/ ke'u shi ka de bzhin du rga shi'i tshad ni dmyigs su myed de/ nam mkha' tshad myed pa'i phyir rga shi'i tshad myed do// rga shi'i tshad myed pa'i phyir shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa tshad myed do// ke'u ni
124b3('bum): sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa tshad myed pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di tshed myed pa ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de ni 'od sder sbyin pa'i
124b4('bum): ro la tu phyind pa'i tshed ni dmyigs su myed do// ke'u shi ka 'di ralta ste dper na nam mkha'i tshed ni dmyigs su myed do// ke'u shi ka de bzhin du sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa'i tshad kyang dmyigs/ 
124b5('bum): su myed de/ nam mkha' tshang byed pa'i phyir sbyin pa'i pha rol d+ha phyi rnyed pa tshad myed do// sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyi rnyed pa chang myed pa'i phyir zhes rab kyi pha rol tu phyi rad pa tshad myed do/ 
124b6('bum): kelu ni ka tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyind pa chad myed pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha ro la tu phyind pa 'ang ched myed pa ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'ulu shi ka de na
124b7('bum): ltar rgyal khrims kyi pha ro la tu phyinang pa'i tshad na dmyigs su byed do// ke'u'i ka 'di sa ste dper na nam mkha'i tshe da dri myigs su byed do// ke'u shi ka de bzhin du tshul khrims kyi pha ro lang du ma pa
124b8('bum): tshar kyang dmyigs su myed do// nam mkha' tshang med pa'i phyir tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyiring pa tshad myed do// tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyind pa char med pa'i phyir shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa chad kyi
127a1('bum): tshad myed pa'i phyir shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa tshad myed do// ke'u shi ka 'og ma dang tha ma myed pa stong pa nyid tshad myed pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnamang khro ba mo thang tu phyin
127a2('bum): 'di cher myed pa ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de 'i 'di ltar thog ma dngo ba ma med pa stong pa nyid kyi tshad ni dmyigs su myed do// ke'u shi ka 'di lta ste dper na nam mkha'i tshad ni dmyigs su myed do// ke'u zhi ke de ba'i
127a3('bum): du thog ma dang tha mu med pa stong pa nyid kyi ched kyang dmyigs su myed de// nam mkha' tshad byed pa'i phyir thog ma dang tha ma phyed pa stong pa nyid tshad myed do// thog sa dang 'a ma myed pa stong pa nyid tshad myed pa'i phyir zhes rab
127a4('bum): kyi pha rol tu phyinang pa tshad myed do// ke'u shi ka dor ba myed pa stong pa nyid tshad myed pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' che/ na po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyind pa 'di tshad myed pa ste// de ci'i phyir
127a5('bum): zhe na ke'u shi ke de ni di ltar dor ba myed pa stong pa nyid kyi tshed ni dmatshigs su myed do// ke'u shi ke 'di lta ste dper na nam mkha'i tshad ni dmyigs su myed do// ke'u shi ka de bzhin du dor ba myed pa stong
127a6('bum): pa nyid kyi che kyang migs su byed de/ nam ma' 'chad byed pa'i phyir dong bgyid pa stong pa nyid tshad myed do// ror bskyed pa stong pa nyid cang med pa'i phyir shes rab kyi pha ro sang tu phyirang pa chad myed do/ ke'uzhi
127a7('bum): rang bzhin stong / tshod med pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi pha rol tu phyinang pa 'di tshad myed pa ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe nag kelu ni ka de ni 'di ltar rang bzhin stong bya nyid

187b1('bum): bi ris kyi sga'i bu dang gsum bcu tha gsus kyi sgra'i bu dang / ma tshe ma'i lha'i bu dang / dka' ldan gyi spre'i bu dang / 'phrul dka'i ske'i bu dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi ske'i bu dang / tshangs ris kyi lga'i bu dang /

262a6('bum): ma myed pa dang smon pa myed pa nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ mngon par shes pa rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ ting nge 'dzind nams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ gzungs kyi sgo rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ de bzhin
262a7('bum): gshegs pa'i stobs rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ myi 'jigs pa rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ so so yang dag par rig rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ snying rje chen po nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ sangs rgyas
262a8('bum): kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ la gcig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ phyir myi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ 
262b1('bum): dgra bcom panye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ rang byang chub nye bar sgrub pa ma yin sas kyi rnam pa zhes pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ rnam pa thams cad mkhye da pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa ma yon no// brgya byin gyis rnam
262b2('bum): pa btsun pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu de de bzhin no// de de bzhin te/ btsun pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu gang gis de ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ so so'i skye bo'i chos rnams
262b3('bum): 'dod par byed pa ma yin/ byang chub sems dpa' chos rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ rang sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ nyan thos kyi chos rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ slob pa dang myi slob pa'i
262b4('bum): chos rnams nye bar sgrub pa yin/ so so'i skye bo'i chos rnams nye bar dasgrub pa ma yin/ 'dus ma byas kyi dbyings nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ 'dus byas kyi khams 'dor bar byed pa ma yin/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu
262b5('bum): phyin pa nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ bzod pa'i pha rold tu phyind pa nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyind pa nye bar
262b6('bum): sgrub pa ma yin/ bami gtan gi pha rol tu phyir pa nye bar sgrub pa ma ma'o// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyirid pa nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ nang stong pa nyid nye bar sgrub pam yin/ phyi stong pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ byin sa
262b7('bum): kha nyid nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ stong pa nyid stong pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ chen po stong pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ don dam pa stong pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa me yin/ 'dus byas stong pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ 
262b8('bum): 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa mi yim/ thog ma dang 'a ma myed pa stong pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa ma yin / dor 'byed pa stong pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa ma yin
263a1('bum): gdang bzhini myong ba nyid nye bar sgrub pam yi ga chos mams cad stong pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ rab kyi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa ma yi ga myi dmyigs pa stong pa nyid nye bar sgrub pam yin / 
263a2('bum): dngos po myed pa stong pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ dngos po myed pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa ma yin// dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ 
263a3('bum): yang dag par spong ba rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ rdzu 'phrul gi rkang pa rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ dbang po rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ stobs rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ byang chub kyi yan lag rnaMs
263a4('bum): nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ bsam rten rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin pa/ tshad myed pa rnaMs
263a5('bum): nye bar sgrub pa ma yin// gzugs myed pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ rnam par tha rad pa rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ mthar kyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnaMs
263a6('bum): nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ rnam par tha rang ba'i sgo stong pa nyid dang mtshan ma myed pa dang smo dang ba myed pa rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ mngon par shes pa rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ ting nge 'dzin rnams nye bar sgrub pa ma hA

263b1('bum): 'ong ba'i 'bras bu nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ dgra bcom pa nyid nye bar sgrub 'am yin/ rab byang chub nye bar smrab bam yin/ las kyi nas bshes pa nyid nye bar sgrub pa ma yin/ rnam pa thams cad mthe na pa nyi
263b2('bum): bar sgrub pa ma yin/ zhes bya bar shes pa de ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la myod pa yin no// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la sgom pa yin no// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa ni gnyis su shes par bya ba ma yin te/ 
263b3('bum): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa ni skyo gnyis pa'o// zas ma ga tan gi pha rol tu phyind pa ni gnyis su shes par bya ba ma yin te/ bsam gtan gi pha rol tu phyind pa ni myo gnyis pa'o// 'artson 'grus kyi pha rol
263b4('bum): tu phyind pa ni gnyis su shes par bya ba ma yin te/ brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyind pa ni myo gnyis pa'o// bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa ni gnyis su shes par bya ba ma yin te/ bzod pa'i pha
263b5('bum): rol tu phyind pa ni myo gnyis pa'o// tshul khrims kyi pha rold tu phyin da pa ni gnyis su shes par bya ba ma yin te// tshul khrims kyi pha ro lad tu phyind pa ni myo gnyis pa'o// sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa
263b6('bum): ni gnyis su zhes par bya ba ma yin te/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyi nad pa ni mya gnyis pa'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis legs so zhes bya ba gnang ste/ ke'u shi ka legs so legs so de de/ 
263b7('bum): bzhin te/ ji skad smras pa de bzhin no// shes rab kyi ma chob da tu byi nga ba ni gnyi su shes par bya ba ma yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ shes rab kyi pha rol da tu phyin pani myi gnyis pam bsam gtan gi sa rol du
263b8('bum): tham gnyis su shes par bya ba ma yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhen pa bamam gtan gi pha rol tu phyind pa ni phyi gnyis pa'o// brtson 'grus kyi pha rolab tu phyirnyed pa ni gnyis su shes par shes par bya ba ma yin te/ de ci
264a1('bum): 'byor zhe rag brtson 'grus kyis rol tu phyind pa myo gnyis pa'o// 'azod pa'i pha romang tu phyind pa ni gnyis su zhes par bya ba ma yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ bzod pa'i pharol pa tu phyin pa
264a2('bum): myi gnyis pa'o// tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyind pa ni kanyi su shes par bya ba ma yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyind pa ni myo gnyis pa'o// sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa ni gnyis su
264a3('bum): zhes par bya ba ma yin te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sbyin pa'i pha rold tu phyind pa myi gnyis pa'o// ke'u shi ka gang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa la gnyis su 'dod pa de ni chos kyi dbyings la gnyis su 'dod du zad do/ 
264a4('bum): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de ni 'di ltar chos kyi dbyings dang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa de la gnyis su myed de gnyis su bya ra myed do// ke'u shi ka kang bsam gtan gi pha rol tu phyin pa la
264a5('bum): gnyis su 'dod pa de ni chos kyi dbyings la gnyis su 'dod du za da do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de ni 'di ltar chos kyi byings dang bsam gtan gi pha rol tu phyind pa de la gnyis su myed de

264a7('bum): rang brtson 'grus kyi pha rolang tu phyird pa de la gnyis su myed de gnyis su byar byed do// ke'u shi ka gang bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa la gnyis su 'dod pa de ni chos kyi dbyings la gnyis su 'dod du zad do//

265a1('bum): tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyind pa dang de bzhin nyid la gnyi su myed de gnyis su byar myed do// ke'u shi ka gang sbyar ba'i pha rol tu phyind pa la gnyi su 'dod pa de ni de bzhin nyid la gnyis su 'dod du zad do// de ci/

266a1('bum): ma pa'i dbyings sa gnyis su 'dod du bang // de ci'i khyim nam/ ke'u zhi ga de ni 'di ltar byin pa'i marol tu byin pa dang bsam gyis gyi khyab pa'i dbyings de la gnyis su myed de gnyis su byar byed do//

336b5('bum): 'phrul dga'i sgra rnams yod do// gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams yod do// tshangs ris kyi lha rnams yod do// tshangs lnga nye phan gi lha rngams yod do// tshangs pa kun 'khor gi lha rnams yod
336b6('bum): do/ tshangs chen gi lha rnams yod do// snang ba'i lha rnams yod do// chung snang gi lha rnams yod do// tshad myed snang ba'i sgra rnams yod do// kun snang dang ba'i lha rnams yod do// dge ba'i lha rnams yod do/ 
336b7('bum): chung dge'i lha rnams yod do// tshad myed dge ba'i lha rnams yod do// dge rgyas kyi lha rnams yod do// che ba'i lha rnams yod do// chung che'i lha rnams yod do// tshad myed che ba'i lha rnams yod do// 'bras bu che ba'i
336b8('bum): lnga rnams yod do// myi che ba'i lha rnams yod do// myi gdung ba'i lha rnams yod do// shi nad tu mthong ba'i lha rnams yod do// gya nom snang ba'i lha rnams yod do// 'og myin gi sde rnams yod do// nam mkha' mtha
337a1('bum): yas skye mched kyi lha rnams yod do// rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched kyi lha rnams yod do// cung zad myed pa'i skye mched kyi lha rnams yod do// 'du shes myed 'du shes myed myin skye mched kyi lha rnams yod do
337a2('bum): sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa yod do// rlul khrims kyi pha rolab tu phyind pa yod do// bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa yod do// brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyind pa yod do// bsam gtan gi pha rol tu phyind pa yod do// 
337a3('bum): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa song ngo // nang stong pa nyid yod do// phyi stong pa nyid yod dog/ phyi nang stong pa nyid yod do/ stong pa nyid stong pa nyid yod do// chen po stong pa nyid yod do// don dam pa stong pa nyid yo na
337a4('bum): 'dus byas stong pa nyid yod do// 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid yod do// mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid yod do// thog ma dang tha ma myed pa stong ba nyid yod do// dor ba myed pa stong pa nyid yod do// rang bzhin stong pa
337a5('bum): nyid yod ngo // chos thams cad stong pa nyid yod do// rang kyi ma tshan nyid stong pa nyid yod do// myi myigs pa stong pa nyid yod ngo/ dngos po myed pa stong pa nyid yod do// ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid yod
337a6('bum): ngo/ dngos po myed pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid yod do// dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams yod do/ yang dag par spong ba rnams yod do// rdzu 'phrul gi rkang pa rnams yod do// dbang po rnams yod do// stobs
337a7('bum): rnams yod do// byang chub kyi yan lag rnams yod do// 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa yod do// 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams yod do// bsam gtan rnams yod do// tshad myed pa rnams yod do/ 
337a8('bum): gzugs myed pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams sod do rnam par b.rad pa 'arkyang yo ngo// mab da kyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug sa gu sod do / gnas par bdad pa'i ni stong pa nyid dngag mtshams byed pa dang / 
337b1('bum): smon dpa myed pa yod do// mngon par shes pa rnams yod do// ting nge 'dzind rnams yod do// gzungs kyi sgo rnams yod do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams yod do// myi 'jigs pa rnams yod do// so so yang dag par
337b2('bum): rig pa rnams yod do// snying rje chen po yod do// sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad yod do// rgyu nad tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu yod do// sun cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu yod do// phyir myi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu yod do// 
337b3('bum): dgra bcom pa rnams yod do// rang byang chub yod do// lam gyi rnam pa zhes pa nyid yod do// rnam pa thams cad mkhyend pa nyid yod do// rgyu nang tu zhugs pa rnams yod do// lan cig phyir 'ong ba rnam nas bayod do// 
337b4('bum): phyir myi 'ong ba rnams yod do// dgra bcom pa rnams yod do// rang sangs rgyas rnams yod do// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpal chen po rnams yod do// de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag
337b5('bum): par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams yod do// ke'u shi ka steng gi phyo/ sa kyi 'jig rte nang gi khams kang ka'i klung gi bye ma snyed kyi sems na ji snyed pa de dag rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo la las bsam rtan
337b6('bum): bzhi la bkod de/ tshad myed pa bzhi dang / gzugs myed pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhi dang / mngon par shes pa lnga la rab tu bkod na/ ke'u shi ka de ji snyam du sems/ rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo de'i bsod nas
337b7('bum): de'i rgyus mang du 'phel lam/ gsol da pa/ bcom ldan 'das mang ngo // bde bar gshegs pa mang ngo // bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' saHla dpa/ ke'u shi ka de bas rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo gang gis shes
337b8('bum): rab kyi pha rold tu phyind pa 'di'i glegs bam bklag pa dang / bri ba dang / kha ton du bya ba'i phyir gzhan byin na/ bsod nams ches mang du 'phel lo// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ke'u shi ka de ni 'di ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu
338a1('bum): phyi nang pa 'di las zag pa myed pa'i chos rnams rgya cher bsta nang te/ de dag la bslabs shing rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo dag yang dag pa'i skyon byed par zhugs par gyur to// 'jug ko 'jug para'/ 
338a2('bum): 'gyur ro// rgyu na tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu thob par gyur to// 'thob po thob par 'gyur ro// lan nig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu 'ol par gyur to// 'thob po 'ob par 'gyur ro// phyir myi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu thob par gyur / 
338a3('bum): to/ 'thob po thob par 'gyur ro// dgra bcos pa nyid thob par gyur da to// 'thob po thob par 'gyur ro// rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa rnams kyis rang byang chub thob par gyur to// 'job bo// thob par 'gyur ro/ 
338a4('bum): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyang byang chub sem sa dpa'i skyon myed par zhugs par gyurard to// 'jug ko 'jug par 'gyur ro// bla na myed pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon
338a5('bum): par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so// mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ro// ke'u shi ka zag pa myed pa'i chos de dag kyang gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ 
338a6('bum): sbyin pa'i pha rold tu phyind pa dang / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyind pa dang / bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyind pa dang / brtson 'grus kyi pha ro lad tu phyind pa dang bsam gtan gi pha rol tu phyind pa dang / 
338a7('bum): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyind pa dang / nang stong pa nyid dang / phyi stong pa nyid dang / phyi nang stong pa nyid dang // stong pa nyid stong pa nyid dang / chen po stong pa nyid dang / don dam pa stong pa nyid dang / 'dus byas stong pa
